		add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
		add_character_flag = sexuality_ensure_heterosexual
	}
	8255.1.1 = { add_spouse = Stark_127 } # Lyarra Stark

	8281.6.1 = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					character:Tully_1 = { is_alive = yes }
					character:Stark_2 = { is_alive = yes }
					character:Tully_4 = { is_alive = yes }
				}
				create_alliance = { # By marriage
					target = character:Tully_1 # Hoster Tully
					allied_through_owner = character:Stark_2 # Brandon Stark
					allied_through_target = character:Tully_4 # Catelyn Tully
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					character:Baratheon_2 = { is_alive = yes }
					character:Stark_5 = { is_alive = yes }
				}
				create_alliance = { # By marriage
					target = character:Baratheon_2 # Robert Baratheon
					allied_through_owner = character:Stark_5 # Lyanna Stark
					allied_through_target = character:Baratheon_2 # Robert Baratheon
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8282.7.9 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_wildfire_killer # Burned alive in his armor
			killer = Targaryen_1 # Aerys II Targaryen
		}

				add_opinion = {
					target = character:Targaryen_3 # Rhaegar Targaryen
					modifier = named_me_queen_of_love_and_beauty_opinion
				}
			}
		}
		create_character_memory = {
			type = agot_named_as_qolab

				set_relation_rival = character:Warrick_7 # Britt Warrick
			}
		}
	}
	8300.1.15 = {
		trait = nightswatch_historical
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { character:Castle_Black_9 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_friend = character:Castle_Black_9 # Finn
			}
			if = {
				limit = { character:Castle_Black_34 = { is_alive = yes } }
				set_relation_friend = character:Castle_Black_34 # Cotter
			}
			agot_join_nightswatch_history_effect = {
				ORDER = ranger
				CASTLE = title:c_castle_black
				NW_JOIN_AGE = 19
			}
		}
	}
}
